function _createMdxContent(props) {
  const _components = {
    a: "a",
    br: "br",
    code: "code",
    em: "em",
    h2: "h2",
    h3: "h3",
    h4: "h4",
    li: "li",
    ol: "ol",
    p: "p",
    pre: "pre",
    strong: "strong",
    table: "table",
    tbody: "tbody",
    td: "td",
    th: "th",
    thead: "thead",
    tr: "tr",
    ul: "ul",
    ..._provideComponents(),
    ...props.components
  };
  return _jsxs(_Fragment, {
    children: [_jsx(_components.h2, {
      id: "data-actions",
      children: "Data Actions"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "createmods",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "create(...mods)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Creates a new bot or combination of bots with the given mods. Also triggers ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onCreate"
      }), " on all the created bots.\nBy default, bots are created with a unique ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "id"
      }), ", ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "creator"
      }), " set to the current ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "bot.id"
      }), ", and ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "space"
      }), " set to ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "shared"
      }), ".\nBots must be created with at least one tag. If ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "create()"
      }), " tries to make a bot with zero tags then an error will be thrown."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["If ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "creator"
      }), " references a non-existent bot or a bot with a different ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "space"
      }), " than the created bot, then ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "creator"
      }), " will be set to ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "null"
      }), "."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: [_jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "Each parameter"
      }), " is a mod that should be applied to the new bot(s).\nIf no parameters are specified, then the new bot will have its ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "creator"
      }), " set to ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "bot.id"
      }), " and ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "space"
      }), " set to ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "shared"
      }), ".\nIf an array of mods is used for a parameter, then one bot will be created for ", _jsx(_components.em, {
        children: "each unique combination of mods"
      }), "."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title=\"Create a red bot\"",
        children: "let myRedBot = create({\n    color: \"red\"\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title=\"Create a parent and a child bot\"",
        children: "let myParentBot = create({\n    creator: null,\n    label: \"Parent\"\n});\nlet myChildBot = create({\n    creator: getID(myParentBot),\n    label: \"Child\"\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title=\"Create a red bot in the tempLocal space\"",
        children: "let myBot = create({ space: \"tempLocal\", color: \"red\" });\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title=\"Create a bot from multiple mods\"",
        children: "// myBot is placed in the \"myDimension\" dimension and is colored green\nlet myBot = create({ myDimension: true }, {\n    color: \"green\"\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title=\"Create a red bot and a blue bot\"",
        children: "let [myRedBot, myBlueBot] = create({ creator: null}, [\n    {\n        \"color\": \"red\"\n    },\n    {\n        \"color\": \"blue\"\n    }\n]);\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "destroybot",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "destroy(bot)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Removes the given bot, list of bots, or bot by ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "id"
      }), " and triggers ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onDestroy"
      }), " for each of the destroyed bots."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Note that only destroyable bots will be destroyed.\nBots that have ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "destroyable"
      }), " set to ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "false"
      }), " will not be destroyed."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Also note that all bots that have ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "creator"
      }), " set to the ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "id"
      }), " of a destroyed bot will also be destroyed (unless they are not destroyable).\nThis happens recursively until there are no more bots to destroy."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-1",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title=\"Destroying a single bot\"",

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title=\"Destroying a list of bots\"",
        children: "// Destroy all the bots that have #color set to \"red\"\ndestroy(getBots(\"#color\", \"red\"));\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title=\"Destroying a bot by its id\"",
        children: "// Destroy the bot with the #id: \"config\"\ndestroy(\"config\");\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {

        children: "applyMod(bot, ...mods)"
      })

    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {

      }), " is the bot that the mods should be applied to."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "other parameters"
      }), " are the mods that should be applied to the bot. If two mods have the same tag, then the mod that is last in the list will win."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-2",

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Removes the tags contained in the given mod(s) from the given bot or mod."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the bot or mod that the tags should be removed from."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "other parameters"

      id: "examples-3",

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {

    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {

      })

        tag: "@[groupName][stateName]OnExit"
      }), " and ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@[groupName][stateName]OnEnter"

      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {

      }), " tag will be used."]

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "getlinkbots",

        children: "getLink(...bots)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {

    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: [_jsx(_components.strong, {

      }), " is the bot or bot ID that should be linked to."]

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

        children: "getBots(..filters)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Gets an array of bots that match all of the given filter(s). The returned array is sorted alphabetically by the ", _jsx(TagLink, {

      }), " tag."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: [_jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "Each parameter"

        href: "#bot-filters",
        children: "bot filter"
      }), ". If no filters are specified, then all bots in the inst are returned.\nIf multiple filters are specified, then only the bots that match all of the filters are returned."]

      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "getBots(tag, value?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Gets an array of bots that match the given tag and value. The returned array is sorted alphabetically by the ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "id"
      }), " tag."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the name of the tag. Bots that have this tag will be included as long as they also match the second parameter."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is the value the tag should match. If not specified, then all bots with the tag will be included.\nIf specified, then only bots that have the same tag and value will be included. If you specify a function as the value, then it will be used to match tag values."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(Alert, {
      type: "info",

        children: "diffSnapshots(first, second)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Calculates the difference between the two given snapshots.\nThe returned value is such that if you were to apply the changes (using ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "applyDiffToSnapshot(snapshot, diff)"
      }), ") it represents to the first snapshot you would end up with the second snapshot."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the snapshot that should be used as the baseline for the diff."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is the snapshot that should be used as the target for the diff."]

      id: "examples-17",

      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "applyDiffToSnapshot(snapshot, diff)"

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Applies the given difference to the given snapshot and returns a new snapshot that represents the result."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"

      }), " class to scripts."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["When you save a DateTime to a tag, CasualOS will automatically format it so that it is automatically detectable as a date and will always be represented the same no matter where in the world you are.\nTo do this, CasualOS uses the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: ""
      }), " emoji as a prefix for date + time values and automatically parses them into DateTime objects."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["For example, saving ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "2022-10-03"
      }), " to the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "date"
      }), " tag will make ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "tags.date"
      }), " be a DateTime value that represents midnight on the 3rd of October in 2022 in the UTC-0 time zone.\nIf you want your date to represend midnight in another time zone, you can add the ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "https://nodatime.org/TimeZones",
        children: "IANA time zone"
      }), " you want to the end of the value.\nThis is midnight in Tokyo: ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "2022-10-03 Asia/Tokyo"
      }), "."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["See ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "https://moment.github.io/luxon/#/tour",
        children: "luxon"
      }), " for more information and examples."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-25",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Toast a specific time in the local timezone'",
        children: "os.toast(DateTime.local(2020, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2));\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Toast a date in a nice relative format to now'",
        children: "os.toast(DateTime.utc(2021, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2).toRelative()); // => '8 months ago'\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",

        children: "const date1 = DateTime.utc(2021, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2);\nconst date2 = DateTime.local(2021, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2);\nconst duration = date1.diff(date2, 'hours');\nos.toast(duration.toHuman()); // => '-4 hours'\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Check if one date is before another date'",
        children: "const date1 = DateTime.utc(2021, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2);\nconst date2 = DateTime.local(2021, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2);\nconst date3 = DateTime.local(2021, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2);\n\n// Is date1 before date2?\nos.toast(date1 < date2); // => 'true'\n\n// Is date2 equal to date3?\nos.toast(date2.toMillis() === date3.toMillis()); // => 'true'\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "getdatetimevalue",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "getDateTime(value)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Attempts to create a new ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "#datetime",
        children: "DateTime"
      }), " object from the given value.\nReturns a DateTime object if successful. Returns null otherwise."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["See ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "#datetime",
        children: "DateTime"
      }), " for more information."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the value that should be converted into a DateTime.\nIf it is a string, then CasualOS will attempt to parse the string.\nIf it is a ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Date",
        children: "Date object"
      }), " then it will be converted to a DateTime by assuming the Date represents the local time zone."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Supported ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601",
        children: "ISO 8601"
      }), " Formats:"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "2022 # Just the year\n2022-05 # Year + Month\n2022-10-03 # Year + Month + Day\n2022-10-03T07:30:00 # Year + Month + Day + Hour + Minute + Second\n2022-10-03T07:30:00Z # Year + Month + Day + Hour + Minute + Second + explicit UTC-0 marker\n2022-10-03T07:30:00.123Z # Year + Month + Day + Hour + Minute + Second + Milisecond + explicit UTC-0 marker\n2022-10-03T07:30:00.123-05:00 # Year + Month + Day + Hour + Minute + Second + -5 hour time offset from UTC-0\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Note that unless a time-zone offset is explicitly specified, the date will always be interpreted as UTC-0 time."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Supported CasualOS-specific formats:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "# ISO-like formats\n2022 # Just the year\n2022-05 # Year + Month\n2022-10-03 # Year + Month + Day\n2022-10-03T07:30:00 # Date + Time (UTC-0 is assumed)\n2022-10-03T07:30:00Z # Date + Time + explicit UTC-0 marker\n2022-10-03T07:30:00.123Z # Date + Time + Milisecond + explicit UTC-0 marker\n2022-10-03T07:30:00.123-05:00 # Date + Time + -5 hour time offset from UTC-0\n\n# CasualOS formats\n2022-10-03T07:30:00 America/New_York # Date + Time + IANA time zone that date was recorded in\n2022-10-03T07:30:00+05:00 America/Chicago # Date + Time + +5 hour time offset from UTC-0 + IANA time zone that date should be displayed in\n2022-10-03T07:30:00+05:00 local # Date + Time + +5 hour time offset from UTC-0 + time zone should be displayed in local time\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-26",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {

      id: "web-actions",

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "webhookoptions",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "web.hook(options)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Sends a HTTP request using the given options."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Returns a Promise that resolves with the following properties:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "{\n    data: any,\n    status: number,\n    statusText: string,\n    headers: any\n}\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is an object with the following properties:"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let options: {\n    /**\n     * The HTTP Method that the request should use.\n     */\n    method: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The URL that the request should be made to.\n     */\n    url: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The headers to include in the request.\n     */\n    headers?: {\n        [key: string]: string;\n    };\n\n    /**\n     * The data to send with the request.\n     */\n    data?: any;\n\n    /**\n     * The shout that should be made when the request finishes.\n     * This is for legacy code. New code should await the returned promise.\n     */\n    responseShout?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The shout that should be made when the request finishes.\n     */\n    responseShout?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The number of retries that should be attempted for the webhook if it fails.\n     * Defaults to 0.\n     */\n    retryCount?: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The HTTP response status codes that should allow the web request to be retried.\n     * Defaults to:\n     *  - 408 - Request Timeout\n     *  - 429 - Too Many Requests\n     *  - 500 - Internal Server Error\n     *  - 502 - Bad Gateway\n     *  - 503 - Service Unavailable\n     *  - 504 - Gateway Timeout\n     *  - 0 - Network Failure / CORS\n     */\n    retryStatusCodes?: number[];\n\n    /**\n     * The number of miliseconds to wait between retry requests.\n     * Defaults to 3000ms (3 seconds).\n     */\n    retryAfterMs?: number;\n};\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-27",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {
        children: ["Send a HTTP GET request to ", _jsx(_components.code, {

      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {

      })

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h2, {
      id: "utility-actions",
      children: "Utility Actions"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "animatetagbot-tag-options",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "animateTag(bot, tag, options)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Animates the tag on the given bot based on the specified parameters.\nReturns a promise that resolves when the animation is finished and throws an error when the animation is canceled.\nThis is useful for gradually changing a tag on a bot over time. For example, moving a bot from point A to point B without teleporting it."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: [_jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "animateTag(bot, tag, options)"
      }), " is fully integrated with tag masks.\nThis lets you animate tag values in the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "tempLocal"
      }), ", ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "local"
      }), ", ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "player"
      }), ", and ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "shared"
      }), " spaces."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the bot or list of bots that the tag should be animated on."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is the tag that should be animated."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "third parameter"
      }), " are the options that should be used to animate the tag.\nIf ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "null"
      }), " is used, then any active animations for the tag on these bots will be canceled.\nIt should be an object with the following properties:"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let options: {\n\n    /**\n     * The value that the animation should start at.\n     * If omitted, then the current tag value will be used.\n     */\n    fromValue?: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The value that the animation should end at.\n     */\n    toValue: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The number of seconds that the animation should take to complete.\n     */\n    duration: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The space that the tag should be animated in.\n     * If not specified, then \"tempLocal\" will be used.\n     * If set to false, then the bot will be edited instead of using tag masks.\n     * Additionally, if the specified space is the same as the space the bot lives in\n     * then the bot will be edited directly.\n     */\n    tagMaskSpace?: 'tempLocal' | 'local' | 'tempShared' | 'shared' | false;\n\n    /**\n     * The time that the animation should start.\n     * Should be the number of miliseconds since January 1st 1970 UTC-0. (e.g. os.localTime or os.agreedUponTime).\n     */\n    startTime?: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The options for easing.\n     * Can be an \"easing type\" or an object that specifies the type and mode.\n     * If an easing type is specified, then \"inout\" mode is used.\n     * If omitted, then \"linear\" \"inout\" is used.\n     * \n     * Can also be a custom function that takes a single parameter and returns a number.\n     * The paramater will be a number between 0 and 1 indicating the progress through the tween.\n     */\n    easing?: 'linear'\n            | 'quadratic'\n            | 'cubic'\n            | 'quartic'\n            | 'quintic'\n            | 'sinusoidal'\n            | 'exponential'\n            | 'circular'\n            | 'elastic' \n            | ((progress: number) => number)\n            | {\n        /**\n         * The type of easing.\n        */\n        type: 'linear'\n            | 'quadratic'\n            | 'cubic'\n            | 'quartic'\n            | 'quintic'\n            | 'sinusoidal'\n            | 'exponential'\n            | 'circular'\n            | 'elastic';\n\n        /**\n         * Whether to apply the easing at the\n         * start (in), end (out), or start and end (inout) of the tween.\n         */\n        mode: 'in' | 'out' | 'inout';\n    }\n};\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-30",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {
        children: ["Animate the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "#count"
        }), " tag from 0 to 1 over 5 seconds."]
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "await animateTag(bot, \"count\", {\n    fromValue: 0,\n    toValue: 1,\n    duration: 5\n});\n\nos.toast(\"Animation finished!\");\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "2",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Run 2 animations in sequence."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "await animateTag(bot, \"homeX\", {\n    fromValue: 0,\n    toValue: 5,\n    duration: 2\n});\n\nawait animateTag(bot, \"homeY\", {\n    fromValue: 0,\n    toValue: 5,\n    duration: 2\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "3",
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {
        children: ["Run an animation while the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "#loop"
        }), " tag is true."]
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "while(tags.loop) {\n    await animateTag(bot, \"homeX\", {\n        fromValue: 0,\n        toValue: 5,\n        duration: 2\n    });\n}\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "4",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Run an animation with a \"bouncy\" easing mode."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "await animateTag(bot, \"homeX\", {\n    fromValue: 0,\n    toValue: 5,\n    duration: 2,\n    easing: {\n        type: \"elastic\",\n        mode: \"out\"\n    }\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "5",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Run an animation with a custom easing function that causes the animation to progress in 10 distinct steps."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "await animateTag(bot, \"homeX\", {\n    fromValue: 0,\n    toValue: 5,\n    duration: 2,\n    easing: (k) => {\n        return Math.floor(k * 10) / 10;\n    }\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "6",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Run an animation that starts in 1 second."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "await animateTag(bot, \"homeX\", {\n    fromValue: 0,\n    toValue: 5,\n    duration: 2,\n    startTime: os.localTime + 1000,\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "7",
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {

          children: "tempShared"

      children: _jsx(_components.code, {

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "animatetagbot-options",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "animateTag(bot, options)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Animates multiple tags on the given bot based on the specified parameters."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["This works similarly to ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "animateTag(bot, tag, options)"
      }), " but instead of providing a tag name, you instead provide an object for the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "fromValue"
      }), " and ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "toValue"
      }), " options which contains the tags that should be animated."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Returns a promise that resolves when the animation is finished and throws an error when the animation is canceled.\nThis is useful for gradually changing a set of tags on a bot over time. For example, moving a bot from point A to point B without teleporting it."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Unlike calling ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "animateTag(bot, tag, options)"
      }), " multiple times, animations started with this function are grouped together.\nThis means that canceling one animation in the group will also cancel the others."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["This function is fully integrated with tag masks.\nThis lets you animate tag values in the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "tempLocal"
      }), ", ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "local"
      }), ", ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "player"
      }), ", and ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "shared"
      }), " spaces."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the bot or list of bots that the tag should be animated on."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " are the options that should be used to animate the tag.\nIt should be an object with the following properties:"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let options: {\n\n    /**\n     * The tags values that the animation should start at.\n     * Each property should be the name of a tag that should be animated.\n     * The values should be the starting values for the tags.\n     */\n    fromValue: object;\n\n    /**\n     * The tag values that the animation should end at.\n     * Each property should be the name of a tag that should be animated.\n     * The values should be the starting values for the tags.\n     */\n    toValue: object;\n\n    /**\n     * The number of seconds that the animation should take to complete.\n     */\n    duration: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The space that the tag should be animated in.\n     * If not specified, then \"tempLocal\" will be used.\n     * If set to false, then the bot will be edited instead of using tag masks.\n     * Additionally, if the specified space is the same as the space the bot lives in\n     * then the bot will be edited directly.\n     */\n    tagMaskSpace?: 'tempLocal' | 'local' | 'tempShared' | 'shared' | false;\n\n    /**\n     * The options for easing.\n     * Can be an \"easing type\" or an object that specifies the type and mode.\n     * If an easing type is specified, then \"inout\" mode is used.\n     * If omitted, then \"linear\" \"inout\" is used.\n     */\n    easing?: 'linear'\n            | 'quadratic'\n            | 'cubic'\n            | 'quartic'\n            | 'quintic'\n            | 'sinusoidal'\n            | 'exponential'\n            | 'circular'\n            | 'elastic' \n            | {\n        /**\n         * The type of easing.\n        */\n        type: 'linear'\n            | 'quadratic'\n            | 'cubic'\n            | 'quartic'\n            | 'quintic'\n            | 'sinusoidal'\n            | 'exponential'\n            | 'circular'\n            | 'elastic';\n\n        /**\n         * Whether to apply the easing at the\n         * start (in), end (out), or start and end (inout) of the tween.\n         */\n        mode: 'in' | 'out' | 'inout';\n    }\n};\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-31",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {
        children: ["Animate the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "#homeX"
        }), " and", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "#homeY"
        }), " tags from 0 to 1 over 5 seconds."]
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "2",

      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {

      }), " is the number of characters that should be deleted."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "fifth parameter"
      }), " is the space that the tag mask is in. If omitted, then the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "tempLocal"
      }), " space will be used."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-40",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Delete the last two characters from a tag mask."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "deleteTagText(bot, \"myTag\", tags.myTag.length - 2, 2);\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "2",
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {
        children: ["Delete the first 3 characters from a tag mask in the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "local"
        }), " space."]
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "deleteTagText(bot, \"myTag\", 0, 3, \"local\");\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h2, {
      id: "bot-filters",
      children: "Bot Filters"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "bytagtag-value",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "byTag(tag, value?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Creates a bot filter that includes bots that have the given tag that matches the given value."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the name of the tag. Bots that have this tag will be included as long as they also match the second parameter."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is the value that the tag should match. If not specified, then all bots with the tag will be included.\nIf specified, then only bots that have the same tag value will be included. If you specify a function as the value, then it will be used to match tag values."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-41",
      children: "Examples"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {

          children: "#name"
        }), " set to \"bob\"."]
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let bots = getBots(byTag(\"#name\", \"bob\"));\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "2",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Find all bots with a height larger than 2."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {

    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {

        children: "Find all bots with the \"test\" tag."

      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let bots = getBots(byTag(\"#test\"));\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {

        children: "byID(id)"

        children: "inDimension(dimension)"

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "atpositiondimension-x-y",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "atPosition(dimension, x, y)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Creates a bot filter that includes bots that are in the given dimension and at the given X and Y position."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["When this filter is used with ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "getBots(...filters)"
      }), ", the returned bots are sorted in the same order that they are stacked.\nThis means that the first bot in the array is at the bottom of the stack and the last bot is at the top of the stack (assuming they're stackable)."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the name of the dimension."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is the X position. That is, the left-right position of the bots in the dimension."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "third parameter"
      }), " is the Y position. That is, the forward-backward position of the bots in the dimension."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-44",
      children: "Examples"

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "instackbot-dimension",

        children: "inStack(bot, dimension)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Creates a bot filter that includes bots in the same stack as the given bot. The given bot will always be included by this filter as long the given bot is in the given dimension."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["When this filter is used with ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "getBots(...filters)"
      }), ", the returned bots are sorted in the same order that they are stacked.\nThis means that the first bot in the array is at the bottom of the stack and the last bot is at the top of the stack (assuming they're stackable)."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"

        children: "front"
      }), ", ", _jsx(_components.code, {

      }), ", ", _jsx(_components.code, {

        children: "not(filter)"

      children: ["Creates a function that includes bots which ", _jsx(_components.em, {

      }), " match the given filter."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h2, {
      id: "event-actions",
      children: "Event Actions"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "shoutname-arg",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "shout(name, arg?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Sends a shout to all bots that are ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "listening"
      }), " and have a ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "listen-tags",
        children: "listen tag"
      }), " for the specified name. Optionally includes a custom ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "that"
      }), " argument.\nAlso triggers ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onListen"
      }), " and ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onAnyListen"
      }), "."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the name of the shout. e.g. Using ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "onClick"
      }), " for the name will trigger all ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onClick"
      }), " listeners."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "that"
      }), " argument to send with the shout. You do not need to specify this parameter if you do not want to."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-52",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {

          children: "@reset"

      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {

      start: "2",

        }), " event with your name:"]
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {

        children: "shout(\"hello\", \"Bob\");\n"

      id: "whisperbot-name-arg",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "whisper(bot, name, arg?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Sends a whisper to the specified bot(s) that are ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "listening"
      }), " and have a ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "listen-tags",
        children: "listen tag"
      }), " for the given name. Optionally includes a custom ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "that"
      }), " argument.\nAlso triggers ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onListen"
      }), " and ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onAnyListen"
      }), "."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the bot, array of bots, bot ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "id"
      }), ", or array of bot ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "id"
      }), " that the whisper should be sent to."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is the name of the whisper. e.g. Using ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "onClick"
      }), " for the name will trigger the ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onClick"
      }), " listener for the specified bots."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "third parameter"
      }), " is the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "that"
      }), " argument to send with the shout. You do not need to specify this parameter if you do not want to."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-53",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {
        children: ["Send a ", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "@reset"
        }), " event to all bots named ", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "Bob"
        }), ":"]
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let bots = getBots(\"#name\", \"Bob\");\nwhisper(bots, \"reset\");\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "2",
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {
        children: ["Send a ", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "@setColor"
        }), " event to ourself:"]
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "whisper(this, \"setColor\", \"red\");\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "priorityshoutevents-arg",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "priorityShout(events, arg?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Shouts to all bots that are ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "listening"
      }), " and have a ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "listen-tags",
        children: "listen tag"
      }), " for the specified events until one of the bots returns a value.\nOptionally includes a custom ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "that"
      }), " argument. Also triggers ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onListen"
      }), " and ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onAnyListen"
      }), " for the bots that the shout was sent to."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "This function is useful when you want to shout but only want one bot to process the shout."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the array of event names that should be shouted. e.g. Using ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "onClick"
      }), " for the name will trigger the ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onClick"
      }), " listener until a bot returns a value."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-54",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

        children: "superShout(name, arg?)"

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Sends a shout to all of the other instances that are loaded."

        children: "superShout(\"hello\");\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "remoteaction-target",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "remote(action, target?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Sends the given action to another remote."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "In CasualOS, all actions are messages which are placed in a queue and processed one at at time."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["For example, the ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "os.toast(message, duration?)"
      }), " action queues a message which, when processed, will show a toast message.\nHowever, before any action is performed, it is run through the ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onAnyAction"
      }), " listener which can decide whether reject an action using ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "action.reject(action)"
      }), ".\nThis lets you write rules for what actions each player is allowed to take."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["There are a couple special cases. First, when you send/receive an action from someone else (i.e. they sent an action to you using the ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "remote(action)"
      }), " function), it won't run by default.\nInstead it is wrapped as a ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "device"
      }), " action and sent to ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onAnyAction"
      }), " for processing. This lets you decide whether to allow players to send messages to each other and what the effect of those messages are.\nIf you want to perform the action, you can use ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "action.perform(action)"
      }), " on the inner device action to queue it for execution."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the action to send."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is optional and is a object specifing which remote to send the action to. If not specified, then the action is sent to the server.\nIf specified, then the action is sent to all remotes that match the given values. If given a string, then the action is sent to the remote with the matching ID."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-56",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {

        className: "language-typescript",

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {

      })

        children: "os.getPublicRecordKey(name)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Requests an ", _jsx(GlossaryRef, {

        children: "access key"
      }), " for the ", _jsx(GlossaryRef, {
        term: "record",
        children: "public record"

    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",

      })

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "osrecorddatarecordkey-address-data-optionsorendpoint",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "os.recordData(recordKey, address, data, optionsOrEndpoint?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Stores the given ", _jsx(GlossaryRef, {
        term: "data-record",
        children: "data"
      }), " in the given ", _jsx(GlossaryRef, {
        term: "record",
        children: "record"
      }), " at the given address.\nIf data already exists at the given address, it will be overwritten."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Returns a promise that resolves with an object that indicates if the request was successful."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the key that should be used to access the record. You can request a record key by using ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "os.getPublicRecordKey(name)"
      }), "."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is the address that the data should be stored at."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "third parameter"
      }), " is the data that should be stored. This can be any value that can be serialized to JSON.\nMust be less than 300KB in size. If you need to store data larger than 300KB, you can use ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "os.recordFile(recordKey, fileData, options?, endpoint?)"
      }), " instead."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "fourth parameter"
      }), " is optional and is the options that should be used to record the data. It has the following structure:"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let options: {\n    /**\n     * The HTTP Endpoint that should be queried.\n     */\n    endpoint?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The policy that should be used for updating the record.\n     * - true indicates that the value can be updated by anyone.\n     * - An array of strings indicates the list of user IDs that are allowed to update the data.\n     */\n    updatePolicy?: true | string[];\n\n    /**\n     * The policy that should be used for deleting the record.\n     * - true indicates that the value can be erased by anyone.\n     * - An array of strings indicates the list of user IDs that are allowed to delete the data.\n     * Note that even if a delete policy is used, the owner of the record can still erase any data in the record.\n     */\n    deletePolicy?: true | string[];\n}\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Alternatively, it can be the HTTP Endpoint of the records website that the data should be recorded to. If omitted, then the preconfigured records endpoint will be used.\nNote that when using a custom endpoint, the record key must be a valid record key for that endpoint."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "The returned object has the following structure:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let result: {\n    /**\n     * Whether the request was successful.\n     */\n    success: boolean;\n\n    /**\n     * The name of the record that the data was stored in.\n     * Not included if the request failed.\n     */\n    recordName?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The address that the data was stored at.\n     * Not included if the request failed.\n     */\n    address?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The error code for failed requests.\n     */\n    errorCode?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The error message for failed requests.\n     */\n    errorMessage?: string;\n};\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-65",
      children: "Examples"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",

        children: "const recordKeyResult = await os.getPublicRecordKey('myRecord');\nif (!recordKeyResult.success) {\n    os.toast(\"Failed to get a record key! \" + recordKeyResult.errorMessage);\n    return;\n}\nconst result = await os.recordData(recordKeyResult.recordKey, 'myAddress', 'myData');\n\nif (result.success) {\n    os.toast(\"Success!\");\n} else {\n    os.toast(\"Failed \" + result.errorMessage);\n}\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "oserasedatarecordkey-address-endpoint",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "os.eraseData(recordKey, address, endpoint?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Erases the ", _jsx(GlossaryRef, {
        term: "data-record",
        children: "data"
      }), " stored at the given address in the given ", _jsx(GlossaryRef, {
        term: "record",
        children: "record"
      }), ".\nReturns a promise that resolves with an object that contains the data (if successful) or information about the error that occurred."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the key that should be used to access the record. You can request a record key by using ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "os.getPublicRecordKey(name)"

positionalAccuracy: number;\n \n     /**\n      * The heading of the device from north in radians.\n      * 0 is true north, Math.PI/2 is east, Math.PI is south and 3/2*Math.PI is west.\n      * This       children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "os.run(script)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Runs the given script.\nThe script will be executed in a separate environment with no ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "bot"
      }), ", ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "tags"
      }), ", ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "this"
      }), ", ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "data"
      }), ", and ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "that"
      }), " variables.\nThis means that you need to use the ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "getBot(...filters)"
      }), " or ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
        action: "getBots(...filters)"
      }), " functions to read bot data."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Returns a promise that resolves with the returned script value after it has been executed."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the script that should be executed."]

      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "osreplacedragbotbotormod",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "os.replaceDragBot(botOrMod)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Replaces the bot that the user is dragging with the given bot or mod."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "If called when the user is not dragging anything, then the given bot or mod will be dragged using the current input method.\nWhen in VR, the current input method is the most recently used VR controller. Otherwise it is the mouse/touchscreen."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the bot or mod that should be dragged.\nIf given a bot while dragging, then that bot's ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onDrag"
      }), " will be skippped but ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onDrop"
      }), " will be called.\nIf given a bot when not dragging, then that bot's ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onDrag"
      }), " and ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onDrop"
      }), " will be called."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-87",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {

        className: "language-typescript",

      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "2",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Drag a mod that makes other bots red."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "os.replaceDragBot({\n    \"color\": \"red\"\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "osenablecustomdragging",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "os.enableCustomDragging()"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Enables \"custom dragging\" for the current bot drag operation."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Custom dragging tells CasualOS to not move the bot to the dragged position.\nInstead, it will calculate where the bot would be dragged and send that information in the ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onDragging"
      }), " and ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onAnyBotDragging"
      }), " listeners."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "This is useful for custom bot dragging behavior like choosing to scale or rotate a bot instead of moving it."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-88",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Enable custom dragging for the current drag operation'",
        children: "os.enableCustomDragging();\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "osadddropsnaptargets",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "os.addDropSnap(...targets)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Specifies a list of snap targets that can be used to position the currently dragged bot."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "If called when the user is not dragging anything, then this function does nothing."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: [_jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "Each parameter"
      }), " is a snap target and can be one of the following values:"]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(PossibleValuesTable, {
      children: [_jsx(PossibleValueCode, {
        value: "ground",
        children: _jsx(_components.p, {
          children: "The bot will snap to the ground plane. (Default when not in VR)"
        })
      }), _jsx(PossibleValueCode, {
        value: "grid",
        children: _jsx(_components.p, {
          children: "The bot will snap to individual grid tiles."
        })
      }), _jsx(PossibleValueCode, {
        value: "face",
        children: _jsx(_components.p, {
          children: "The bot will snap the faces of other pointable bots."
        })
      }), _jsx(PossibleValueCode, {
        value: "bots",
        children: _jsx(_components.p, {
          children: "The bot will snap to other pointable bots."
        })
      }), _jsx(PossibleValue, {
        value: "A snap point object",
        children: _jsx(_components.p, {
          children: "The bot will snap to the specified position when dragged within the specified distance."
        })
      }), _jsx(PossibleValue, {
        value: "A snap axis object",
        children: _jsx(_components.p, {
          children: "The bot will snap to the specified axis when dragged within the specified distance.\nCurrently not supported on the map portal."
        })
      })]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Snap point objects should have the following form:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let snapPoint: {\n    /**\n     * The position that the bot should be snapped to.\n     */\n    position: { x: number, y: number, z: number };\n\n    /**\n     * The distance that the bot should be from the position in order to snap to it.\n     */\n    distance: number;\n};\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Snap axis objects should have the following form:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let snapAxis: {\n    /**\n     * The direction that the axis travels along.\n     */\n    direction: { x: number, y: number, z: number };\n\n    /**\n     * The center point that the axis travels through.\n     */\n    origin: { x: number, y: number, z: number };\n\n    /**\n     * The distance that the bot should be from any \n     * point along the axis in order to snap to it.\n     */\n    distance: number;\n};\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-89",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Snap the dragged bot to the grid."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "os.addDropSnap(\"grid\");\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "2",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Snap the dragged bot to other bot faces."

      children: _jsx(_components.code, {

      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "4",

      }), "\n"]

      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "5",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Snap the dragged bot to the center or bot faces."

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {

      }), "/", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onDropExit"
      }), "),\nthe specified snap targets will take effect."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "other parameters"

      }), _jsx(PossibleValueCode, {
        value: "grid",
        children: _jsx(_components.p, {
          children: "The bot will snap to individual grid tiles."
        })

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "osadddropgridtargets",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "os.addDropGrid(...targets)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Specifies a list of grids that can be used to position the currently dragged bot."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "If called when the user is not dragging anything, then this function does nothing."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: [_jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "Each parameter"
      }), " is an object with the following properties:"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let grid: {\n    /**\n     * The 3D position that the grid should appear at.\n     */\n    position?: { x: number, y: number, z: number };\n\n    /**\n     * The 3D rotation that the grid should appear at.\n     */\n    rotation?: { x: number, y: number, z: number, w?: number };\n\n    /**\n     * The bot that defines the portal that the grid should exist in.\n     * \n     * If null, then this defaults to the bot that is showing the portal that the dragged bot exists in.\n     * For common cases this will be the configBot, but it could also be a bot that has a portal form.\n     */\n    portalBot?: Bot | string;\n\n    /**\n     * The tag that the portal uses to determine which dimension to show.\n     * Defaults to formAddress if the specified portalBot is not the configBot and gridPortal if the specified portalBot is the configBot.\n     */\n    portalTag?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The 2D bounds of the grid.\n     * Defaults to 10 x 10.\n     */\n    bounds?: { x: number, y: number };\n\n    /**\n     * The priority that this grid should be evaluated in over other grids.\n     * Higher priorities will be evaluated before lower priorities.\n     */\n    priority?: number;\n\n    /**\n     * Whether to visualize the grid while a bot is being dragged.\n     * Defaults to false.\n     */\n    showGrid?: boolean;\n\n    /**\n     * The type of grid that this snap grid should be.\n     * Defaults to the type of grid that the portal bot uses.\n     * \n     * - \"grid\" indicates that the snap target should be a flat grid.\n     * - \"sphere\" indicates that the snap target should be a sphere.\n     */\n    type?: 'grid' | 'sphere';\n};\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-91",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Add a grid for the portal that the bot currently exists in.'",

      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {

    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Add a grid for a specific portal bot.'",
        children: "os.addDropGrid({\n    portalBot: getBot(byTag('form', 'portal'), byTag('formAddress', 'myDimension')),\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Add a grid with a custom size.'",
        children: "os.addDropGrid({\n    position: { x: 0, y: 0, z: 3 },\n    bounds: { x: 20, y: 10 }\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Add a grid that the user can see.'",
        children: "os.addDropGrid({\n    position: { x: 0, y: 0, z: 3 },\n    showGrid: true\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Add multiple grids with custom priorities'",
        children: "os.addDropGrid({\n    position: { x: 0, y: 0, z: 3 },\n    bounds: { x: 10, y: 10 },\n    showGrid: true,\n    priority: 10\n}, {\n    position: { x: 0, y: 0, z: 0 },\n    bounds: { x: 20, y: 20 },\n    showGrid: true,\n    priority: 20\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Add a spherical grid that the user can see.'",
        children: "os.addDropGrid({\n    type: \"sphere\",\n    position: { x: 0, y: 0, z: 3 },\n    showGrid: true\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "osaddbotdropgridbot-targets",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "os.addBotDropGrid(bot, ...targets)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Specifies a list of grids that can be used to position the currently dragged bot when it is being dropped on the given bot."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "If called when the user is not dragging anything, then this function does nothing."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the bot which, when the dragged bot is being dropped onto it (as indicated by ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onDropEnter"
      }), "/", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "@onDropExit"
      }), "),\nthe specified snap targets will take effect."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "other parameters"
      }), " are objects with the following properties:"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let grid: {\n    /**\n     * The 3D position that the grid should appear at.\n     */\n    position?: { x: number, y: number, z: number };\n\n    /**\n     * The 3D rotation that the grid should appear at.\n     */\n    rotation?: { x: number, y: number, z: number, w?: number };\n\n    /**\n     * The bot that defines the portal that the grid should exist in.\n     * \n     * If null, then this defaults to the bot that is showing the portal that the dragged bot exists in.\n     * For common cases this will be the configBot, but it could also be a bot that has a portal form.\n     */\n    portalBot?: Bot | string;\n\n    /**\n     * The tag that the portal uses to determine which dimension to show.\n     * Defaults to formAddress if the specified portalBot is not the configBot and gridPortal if the specified portalBot is the configBot.\n     */\n    portalTag?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The 2D bounds of the grid.\n     * Defaults to 10 x 10.\n     */\n    bounds?: { x: number, y: number };\n\n    /**\n     * The priority that this grid should be evaluated in over other grids.\n     * Higher priorities will be evaluated before lower priorities.\n     */\n    priority?: number;\n\n    /**\n     * Whether to visualize the grid while a bot is being dragged.\n     * Defaults to false.\n     */\n    showGrid?: boolean;\n\n    /**\n     * The type of grid that this snap grid should be.\n     * Defaults to the type of grid that the portal bot uses.\n     * \n     * - \"grid\" indicates that the snap target should be a flat grid.\n     * - \"sphere\" indicates that the snap target should be a sphere.\n     */\n    type?: 'grid' | 'sphere';\n};\n"
      })

      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "os.tip(message, pixelX?, pixelY?, duration?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Shows a temporary \"tooltip\" message on the screen. Optionally placed at the specified position and shown for the given duration.\nReturns a promise that resolves with the ID of the new tooltip."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "If a position is not specified, then a position just below the current mouse position will be used. If on mobile, then the last touch position will be used or the center of the screen if the user has not touched the screen.\nAdditionally, if a position is not specified then the tooltip will be automatically hidden if the user moves the mouse significantly away from the position that the mouse was at when the tooltip was shown."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the text that the tooltip message should show."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is optional and is the horizontal pixel position that the tooltip should be shown at on the screen. If not specified then the current mouse position will be used."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "third parameter"
      }), " is optional and is the vertical position that the tooltip should be shown at on the screen. If not specified then a position just below the current mouse position will be used."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "fourth parameter"
      }), " is optional and is the number of seconds that the toast should be shown for before automatically being hidden. (Default is 2)"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-102",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Show a \"Hello!\" tip message."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "os.tip(\"Hello!\");\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "2",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Show a tip at the center of the screen."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "os.tip(\"This is in the center of the screen.\", gridPortalBot.tags.pixelWidth / 2, gridPortalBot.tags.pixelHeight / 2);\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "3",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Show a tip near the mouse cursor for 5 seconds."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "os.tip(\"5 second tip.\", null, null, 5);\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "4",

        children: "os.hideTips(tipIDs?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Hides the tooltips that have the specified IDs. If no arguments are specified, then all tooltips will be hidden.\nReturns a promise that resolves when the tooltips have been hidden."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the tooltip ID or array of tooltip IDs that should be hidden."]

      id: "examples-103",

    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {

      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "const id = await os.tip(\"Hello!\");\nawait os.sleep(1000);\nawait os.hideTips(id);\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "osfocusonbotorposition-options",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "os.focusOn(botOrPosition, options?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Focuses on the given bot or position.\nFor bots in the bot or miniGridPortals, this animates the camera such that the portal focus point is placed on the given bot or position.\nFor input bots in menu portal, this gives keyboard focus to them."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Returns a promise which resolves when the bot has been focused.\nFor the bot and miniGridPortals this is when the animation finishes and rejects if the user takes control of the camera during the animation.\nFor menu bots this is when the input field is focused and rejects if the bot is not a input bot."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the bot, bot ID, or position that should be focused. If null, then the current focus animation will be canceled."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is optional and can be used to specify additional details about how the camera should be animated.\nIt should be an object with the following properties:"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "let options: {\n    /*\n    * The zoom value to use.\n    * For the bot and miniGridPortals, possible values are between `0` and `80`. `1` is the default.\n    * For the map portal, this is the scale that the focused point should appear at.\n    * For example, 24000 would indicate that the scale is 1:24,000.\n    * If no value is specified, then the zoom will remain at its current value.\n    */\n    zoom?: number;\n\n    /*\n     * The rotation value to use in radians.\n     * These are the polar coordinates that determine where\n     * the camera should orbit around the target point.\n     */\n    rotation?: {\n        x: number;\n        y: number;\n\n        /**\n         * Whether to normalize the rotation. Normalized rotations are clamped to between 0 and Math.PI*2.\n         * You can set this to false to allow using angles more than Math.PI*2. This would allow the camera to rotate around an object multiple times.\n         * Defaults to true.\n         */\n        normalize?: boolean;\n    };\n\n    /**\n     * The duration in seconds that the animation should take.\n     * Defaults to 1.\n     */\n    duration?: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The portal that the bot should be focused in.\n     * If not specified, then the bot will be focused in all the portals it is in. (bot, mini and menu)\n     * Useful if a bot is in two portals but you only want to focus it in one portal.\n     */\n    portal?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The tag that should be focused.\n     * Only supported in the system portal.\n     */\n    tag?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The tag space that should be focused.\n     * Only supported in the system portal, sheet portal, and tag portals.\n     */\n    space?: string;\n\n    /**\n     * The line number that should be selected in the editor.\n     * Only supported in the system portal, sheet portal, and tag portals.\n     */\n    lineNumber?: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The column number that should be selected in the editor.\n     * Only supported in the system portal, sheet portal, and tag portals.\n     */\n    columnNumber?: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The index of the first character that should be selected.\n     * Only supported in the system portal, sheet portal, and tag portals.\n     */\n    startIndex?: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The index of the last character that should be selected.\n     * Only supported in the system portal, sheet portal, and tag portals.\n     */\n    endIndex?: number;\n\n    /**\n     * The options for easing.\n     * Can be an \"easing type\" or an object that specifies the type and mode.\n     * If an easing type is specified, then \"inout\" mode is used.\n     * If omitted, then \"quadratic\" \"inout\" is used.\n     */\n    easing?: 'linear'\n            | 'quadratic'\n            | 'cubic'\n            | 'quartic'\n            | 'quintic'\n            | 'sinusoidal'\n            | 'exponential'\n            | 'circular'\n            | 'elastic' \n            | {\n        /**\n         * The type of easing.\n        */\n        type: 'linear'\n            | 'quadratic'\n            | 'cubic'\n            | 'quartic'\n            | 'quintic'\n            | 'sinusoidal'\n            | 'exponential'\n            | 'circular'\n            | 'elastic';\n\n        /**\n         * Whether to apply the easing at the\n         * start (in), end (out), or start and end (inout) of the tween.\n         */\n        mode: 'in' | 'out' | 'inout';\n    }\n}\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["See ", _jsx(TagLink, {
        tag: "portalCameraRotationX"
      }), " for more information on polar coordinates."]

    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
