      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "3",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Load a file named \"book.txt\" and toast the contents."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "const result = await server.loadFile('book.txt');\nos.toast(result.data);\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "serversavefilepath-data-options",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "server.saveFile(path, data, options?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Saves a file at the given path with the given data.\nIf the file already exists, then the options are used to determine if the file should be overwritten. By default the file will not be overwritten."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Note that on a Raspberry PI, all USB storage devices are mapped into the ", _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "/drives"
      }), " directory based on the port they were plugged into.\nSaving a file to a USB drive is as simple as specifying the file name.\nIf multiple USB drives are plugged in and a drive is not specified, then the file will be saved to the first drive."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Returns a promise that resolves when the file has been saved."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the path that the file should be saved to. This is usually just the full name of the file to save. (name + file extension)"]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is the data that should be saved into the file."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "third parameter"
      }), " are the options that should be used for saving the file."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(Alert, {
      type: "info",
      children: _jsxs(_components.p, {
        children: ["By default, saving files is disabled on a server.\nTo enable it, you have to write a custom ", _jsx(TagLink, {
          tag: "@onAnyAction"
        }), " listener on the config bot and run an ", _jsx(ActionLink, {
          action: "action.perform(action)"
        }), "."]
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-334",
      children: "Examples:"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {
        children: ["Save a file named \"book.txt\" and trigger a ", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "@onBookSaved"
        }), " shout when it is saved."]
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "server.saveFile('book.txt', 'My memoirs', {\n    callbackShout: 'onBookSaved'\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "2",
      children: ["\n", _jsxs(_components.li, {
        children: ["Save a file named \"book.txt\" to drive ", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "2"
        }), " and trigger a ", _jsx(_components.code, {
          children: "@onBookSaved"
        }), " shout when it is loaded."]
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "server.saveFile('/2/book.txt', 'My memoirs', {\n    callbackShout: 'onBookSaved',\n    overwriteExistingFile: true\n});\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      start: "3",
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Save a file named \"book.txt\" and send a toast when it is finished."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "await server.saveFile('/2/book.txt', 'My memoirs', {\n    overwriteExistingFile: true\n});\n\nos.toast(\"File Saved!\");\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h2, {
      id: "admin-actions",
      children: "Admin Actions"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "adminspaceunlockpassword",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "adminSpace.unlock(password)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Unlocks the admin space using the given password.\nReturns a Promise that resolves once the space is unlocked.\nThe promise will be rejected if the space was unable to be unlocked."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "If given the correct password, admin space will be unlocked and become editable."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the password that should be used to unlock admin space."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-335",
      children: "Examples"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Unlock admin space."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "try {\n    await adminSpace.unlock(\"my-password\");\n    os.toast(\"Admin Space Unlocked!\");\n} catch(err) {\n    os.toast(\"Failed to unlock admin space \" + err);\n}\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "adminspacesetpasswordoldpassword-newpassword",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "adminSpace.setPassword(oldPassword, newPassword)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "Sets the password that should be used to unlock admin space.\nReturns a Promise that resolves once the password is changed."
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.p, {
      children: "If given the correct password, admin space will use the new password."
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the password that is currently used to unlock admin space."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is the password that should be used to unlock admin space."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-336",
      children: "Examples"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.ol, {
      children: ["\n", _jsx(_components.li, {
        children: "Change the admin space password."
      }), "\n"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        children: "try {\n    await adminSpace.setPassword(\"old-password\", \"new-password\");\n    os.toast(\"Admin Space Password Changed!\");\n} catch(err) {\n    os.toast(\"Failed to change the password \" + err);\n}\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h2, {
      id: "analytics-actions",
      children: "Analytics Actions"
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Analytics actions are actions that record events to ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "https://www.simpleanalytics.com/",
        children: "Simple Analytics"
      }), "."]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h3, {
      id: "analyticsrecordeventname-metadata",
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        children: "analytics.recordEvent(name, metadata?)"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["Records the given event to Simple Analytics using their ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "https://docs.simpleanalytics.com/events",
        children: "Events API"
      }), ".\nReturns a promise that resolves when the event has been recorded."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "first parameter"
      }), " is the name of the event that should be recorded. Must consist of ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "https://docs.simpleanalytics.com/events#valid-event-names",
        children: "only alphanumeric characters and underscores"
      }), "."]
    }), "\n", _jsxs(_components.p, {
      children: ["The ", _jsx(_components.strong, {
        children: "second parameter"
      }), " is optional and should be an object containing the metadata that should be collected with the event. (See ", _jsx(_components.a, {
        href: "https://docs.simpleanalytics.com/metadata",
        children: "metadata"
      }), " for more information)"]
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.h4, {
      id: "examples-337",
      children: "Examples"
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Record an analytics event'",
        children: "await analytics.recordEvent('my_event');\n"
      })
    }), "\n", _jsx(_components.pre, {
      children: _jsx(_components.code, {
        className: "language-typescript",
        metastring: "title='Record an analytics event with some metadata'",
        children: "await analytics.recordEvent('my_event', {\n    myNumber: 1\n});\n"
      })
    })]
  });
}
export default function MDXContent(props = {}) {
  const {wrapper: MDXLayout} = {
    ..._provideComponents(),
    ...props.components
  };
  return MDXLayout ? _jsx(MDXLayout, {
    ...props,
    children: _jsx(_createMdxContent, {
      ...props
    })
  }) : _createMdxContent(props);
}
